Hint EXTRA4.1.Consider the hyperbola \frac{x^2}{a^2}-\frac{y^2}{b^2}=1. Construct a box centered at the origin with corners at (a, \pm b) and (-a,\pm b). Draw lines through the diagonals of this box. Rewrite the equation of the hyperbola by solving for y and then factoring to show that as x gets large, the hyperbola gets really close to the lines y=\pm \frac{b}{a}x.
